### System — 2026-07-01T22:29:44.819276

[Compressed Memory Summary]
The following is a compressed summary of earlier conversation turns, replacing the raw transcript to stay within the context window.

**Task:** Perform a deep‑dive market research on the perpetual futures instrument **TAC‑USDT**. Use the full suite of Blofin analysis tools (ticker, candles, technical analysis, funding rate, news search, universe snapshot, rank opportunities, position‑size computation, etc.) to evaluate the instrument. Produce a single JSON object containing:

- `suggested_side` (buy or sell)  
- `move_potential_pct` (estimated % price move)  
- `confidence` (high/medium/low)  
- `veto` (true if a strong reason to avoid the trade)  
- `thesis` (concise rationale, emphasizing asymmetric upside)

**Constraints / Guidance**
- Focus on asymmetric upside potential.  
- Leverage all relevant data sources (price, volume, momentum, funding, news sentiment, technical indicators).  
- Ensure any open positions are protected (TP/SL) if later execution is needed, but the immediate output is the research JSON.  
- No redundant calls; gather only needed information to form the thesis.

### Key Insights
- **Strong Downward Move:** TAC has fallen ~34 % in the past 24 h, from an open of 0.0628 USDT to a current price of 0.0415 USDT.
- **High Volatility Potential:** The 24 h range (0.039996 – 0.065626) is a ~65 % swing, indicating the token can move sharply—useful for asymmetric payoff setups.
- **Liquidity:** 24 h volume is ~23 M USDT (≈ 234 k TAC). Order‑book depth at the top is thin (1–2 TAC), suggesting larger market orders could move price noticeably.
- **Current Market Tightness:** Bid‑ask spread is tiny (≈ 0.000011 USDT, ~0.03 % of price), so entry/exit slippage is minimal for small orders, but larger orders may impact price due to shallow depth.

### Potential Trading Considerations
1. **Momentum Play:** The steep decline may set up a short‑bias continuation or a rebound bounce. Verify recent order‑flow or news for catalyst.
2. **Risk‑Reward:** With a 24 h high of 0.0656, a short target near that level could give >3.6 % upside on a short entry near the current price, meeting the 3:1 R:R requirement.
3. **Funding Rate & Open Interest:** Retrieve funding data and open‑interest to confirm bias (e.g., negative funding would favor shorts).
4. **Technical Confirmation:** Run `blofin_technical_analysis` for TAC‑USDT to check trend indicators, support/resistance, and momentum oscillators before committing.
